# ADR-358 ŌĆö DXF Stair Tool: Google-Level Parametric Staircase System

**Status**: ­¤¤Ī PROPOSED (round 2 in corso ŌĆö Q1-Q16 risolti, Q17+ in Q&A)
**Date**: 2026-05-16
**Category**: Drawing System / DXF Viewer
**Author**: Giorgio Pagonis + Claude (Opus 4.7)
**Related ADRs**: ADR-031, ADR-032, ADR-040, ADR-055, ADR-057, ADR-186, ADR-195, ADR-294, ADR-340, ADR-343, ADR-344, ADR-345, ADR-353, ADR-357, ADR-GEOMETRY

---

## 1. Context

L'app `Nestor_Pagonis` ha un subapp **DXF Viewer** (editor di k├Ītopsi / floor plan) con architettura matura: ribbon (ADR-345), tool state SSoT (ADR-055), command pipeline (ADR-031/057), micro-leaf preview (ADR-040), parametric Array Entity (ADR-353), line tool Google-level (ADR-357). Manca completamente il **disegno di scale**, una delle primitive base di ogni software architettonico professionale.

Giorgio chiede:
1. Tool che **disegna** scale in pianta.
2. Tool che **calcola automaticamente** lunghezze, larghezze, pedate, alzate.
3. **Tipologie multiple**: rettilinea, circolare, a ╬ō (gamma greco), a ╬Ā (pi greco) / U, ellittica, triangolare.
4. **Pronto per 3D futuro** (oggi solo 2D, ma il modello dati deve essere 3D-ready).
5. **Enterprise / Google-level**: SSoT puro, zero duplicati, riuso massimo dei sistemi centralizzati esistenti.

Questo ADR ├© il contratto architetturale del sistema scale: industry research cross-vendor, codice greco ╬Ø╬¤╬Ü + Eurocode + IBC, gap analysis, modello dati parametrico, pipeline tool, fasi di rilascio, testing.

---

## 2. Background ŌĆö Stato attuale (codice = source of truth, 2026-05-16)

### 2.1 Cosa c'├© gi├Ā (SSoT riusabile)

| SSoT | File | Ruolo per Stair |
|---|---|---|
| `ToolStateStore` | `src/subapps/dxf-viewer/stores/ToolStateStore.ts` | activeTool SSoT ŌĆö aggiungere `'stair'` al union |
| `TOOL_DEFINITIONS` | `src/subapps/dxf-viewer/systems/tools/ToolStateManager.ts` | metadata tool ŌĆö nuova entry `'stair'` con `category:'drawing'`, `requiresCanvas:true`, `supportsDynamicInput:true` |
| `DrawingStateMachine` | `core/state-machine/DrawingStateMachine.ts` | FSM IDLEŌåÆCOLLECTINGŌåÆCOMPLETING (ADR-032) |
| `useDrawingHandlers` + `useUnifiedDrawing` | `hooks/drawing/` | Entry point click/hover, gi├Ā wired a snap+polar+ortho |
| `completeEntity` | `hooks/drawing/completeEntity.ts` | Pipeline unificato creazione entity (ADR-057) |
| `CreateEntityCommand` + `CommandHistory` | `core/commands/` | Undo/redo (ADR-031) |
| `ProSnapEngineV2` | `snapping/global-snap-engine.ts` | 17 snap engines |
| `PreviewCanvas` | `canvas-v2/preview-canvas/PreviewCanvas.tsx` | Rubber-band zero-lag (ADR-040) |
| `RIBBON_PANELS_CONFIG` | `ui/ribbon/data/home-tab-draw.ts` | Split-button con varianti (ADR-345) |
| `ArrayEntity` pattern (parametric) | `types/entities.ts` + `systems/array/` | **Template diretto**: `kind` + `params` ŌåÆ ricomputa geometria. Stair segue stesso pattern. |
| Geometry helpers | `rendering/entities/shared/` + `utils/geometry/` | Arc 3-point, distance, angoli, vettori, area poligono |
| Path arc-length sampler | `systems/array/path-arc-length-sampler.ts` | Sampling equidistante curve ŌĆö riusabile per alzate lungo walkline |
| Building Code engine | `src/services/building-code/` (ADR-186) | Gate-runner ŌĆö punto di estensione per `gate-stair-checker` |
| Enterprise IDs | `src/services/enterprise-id.service.ts` | Aggiungere prefisso `STAIR: 'stair'` |
| i18n locales | `src/i18n/locales/{el,en}/tool-hints.json` + `dxf-viewer.json` | Namespace `tools.stair.*` |

### 2.2 Cosa manca (gap rispetto allo standard CAD)

- ŌØī `StairEntity` nel discriminated union di `Entity`.
- ŌØī Helper geometrici per **spirale archimedea**, **elica**, **ellisse arc-length**, **involuta**, **offset/parallel curve** (per stringers interni/esterni).
- ŌØī **Walkline** (linea di percorso a 300 mm dal corrimano interno).
- ŌØī **Regole NOK/Eurocode per scale** (alzata 14-20 cm, pedata 26-32 cm, formula 2R+G=63).
- ŌØī **Property panel** post-creazione per editing parametrico.
- ŌØī **Separazione params ŌåÆ computed geometry** per building elements (oggi solo ArrayEntity, ed ├© una modifier).

## 3. Industry Benchmark (2026-05-16 cross-vendor research)

### 3.1 Feature convergence ŌĆö Stair Types supportati

| Tool | Straight | L (┬╝) | U / ╬Ā (┬Į) | ╬ō (3 flights) | Spiral | Helical | Elliptical | Winders | Custom sketch |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| AutoCAD Architecture | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | ŌØī | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ |
| Revit 2026 | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | ŌØī (Grasshopper) | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ Sketch |
| ArchiCAD | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ | Ō£ģ 4 winder methods | Ō£ģ |
| Vectorworks | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ U/O | ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ | ŌØī | Ō£ģ Fixed-angle | Ō£ģ Vertex |
| Allplan SmartParts | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ ┬╝ | Ō£ģ ┬Į | Ō£ģ double ┬╝ | Ō£ģ | ŌØī | ŌØī | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ Wizard |
| BricsCAD BIM | Ō£ģ | Ō£ģ L | Ō£ģ C | ŌØī | ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ | ŌØī | ŌØī | ŌØī | ŌØī |

**Convergenza**: tutti supportano Straight + L + U + Spiral + Winders. **Helical + Elliptical** sono premium (Revit/ArchiCAD/Vectorworks nativi).

### 3.2 Parametri standard (industry convergence)

| Param | Significato | Default industry | Range valido | Unit├Ā |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **rise** (alzata / Žü╬»ŽćŽä╬╣) | altezza singolo gradino | 175 mm | IBC 102-178, NOK 140-200 | mm |
| **tread / going** (ŽĆ╬¼Žä╬Ę╬╝╬▒) | profondit├Ā orizzontale | 280 mm | IBC Ōēź279, NOK 260-320 | mm |
| **nosing** (╬╝ŽŹŽä╬Ę) | sporgenza | 25 mm | 0-32 | mm |
| **width** (ŽĆ╬╗╬¼Žä╬┐Žé) | larghezza utile | 1000 mm | NOK Ōēź80, Ōēź120 main | mm |
| **stepCount** | numero alzate | 2-16 per flight | Ōēź3 | int |
| **totalRise** | h piano-piano | = rise ┬Ę stepCount | da quota interpiano | mm |
| **totalRun** | sviluppo planar | = tread ┬Ę (stepCountŌłÆ1) | ŌĆö | mm |
| **headroom** | h libera sopra walkline | Ōēź2000 mm | NOK Ōēź220 | mm |
| **pitch / slope** | angolo | 30-35┬░ | Ōēż45┬░ codice | gradi |
| **walkline offset** | dist walkline da bordo | 300 mm | varia | mm |
| **handrail height** | h corrimano | 900 mm | NOK 90-110 cm | mm |
| **landing depth** (ŽĆ╬╗╬▒ŽäŽŹŽā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐) | profondit├Ā pianerottolo | Ōēźwidth | NOK Ōēź pedata | mm |
| **winder turn angle** | angolo winder | 90┬░ / 180┬░ | ŌĆö | gradi |
| **inner/outer radius** | raggi scale curve | inner Ōēź150 mm | NOK Ōēź15 cm | mm |

### 3.3 Formule comfort/sicurezza

```
Blondel (NOK + Eurocode):  2R + G = 600ŌĆō630 mm
Safety:                    R + G  Ōēł 460 mm
Comfort (difference):      G ŌłÆ R  Ōēł 120 mm
Pitch:                     tan(╬▒) = R / G        (╬▒ ottimale 30-35┬░)
Walkline arc length:       L_walk = (R_inner + walklineOffset) ┬Ę ╬Ė_total
```

### 3.4 Codice edilizio greco (╬Ø╬¤╬Ü ╬Ø.4067/2012 + ╬åŽü╬ĖŽü╬┐ 13 ╬ō╬¤╬Ü)

| Parametro | NOK / GOK |
|---|---|
| Alzata (R) | 14-20 cm; **max 18 cm** ╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒ |
| Pedata (G) | 26-32 cm; **min 25 cm** ╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒ |
| Larghezza (W) | Ōēź80 cm ╬┤╬ĄŽģŽä╬ĄŽü╬ĄŽŹ╬┐ŽģŽā╬▒, Ōēź120 cm ╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒, 110 cm uscite emergenza |
| ╬Ā╬╗╬▒ŽäŽŹŽā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ | profondit├Ā Ōēź W |
| ╬Ü╬▒╬Ė╬▒ŽüŽī ŽŹŽł╬┐Žé | Ōēź220 cm sopra walkline |
| Uniformit├Ā | tutte R uguali, tutte G uguali |
| ╬Ü╬┐ŽģŽĆ╬▒ŽāŽä╬« | obbligatoria se Ōēź3 gradini o W >120 cm |

### 3.5 Codici edilizi ŌĆö tabella comparativa estesa (round 2 research)

| Codice | Rise (mm) | Tread (mm) | Width (mm) | Headroom (mm) | Var. max | Note |
|--------|-----------|-----------|-----------|---------------|---------|------|
| NOK ╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒ (GR) | 140-180 | 260-320 | Ōēź1200 | Ōēź2200 | uniform | ╬Ø.4067/2012 |
| NOK ╬┤╬ĄŽģŽä╬ĄŽü╬ĄŽŹ╬┐ŽģŽā╬▒ (GR) | 140-200 | 250-320 | Ōēź900 | Ōēź2200 | uniform | ŌĆö |
| IBC residential (US) | Ōēż197 | Ōēź254 | Ōēź914 | Ōēź2032 | ŌĆö | IRC R311 |
| IBC commercial (US) | 102-178 | Ōēź279 | Ōēź1118 | Ōēź2032 | ŌĆö | IBC ┬¦1011 |
| NFPA 101 (US) | Ōēż178 | Ōēź279 | Ōēź914 | ŌĆö | Ōēż4.8 mm | Life Safety Code |
| NBC Canada | 125-200 | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | Ōēź2050 | Ōēż5 mm | NBC 2020 |
| AS 1657 (AU industrial) | 130-225 | 240-355 | Ōēź600 | ŌĆö | Ōēż5 mm | 26.5┬░-45┬░ |
| DIN 18065 (DE) | Ōēż200 | Ōēź230 | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | 2R+G=61-65 cm | Blondel |
| Eurocode 2 | structural | structural | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | RC 3-5 kN/m┬▓ |
| ADA / ICC A117.1 | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | Ōēż4.8 mm | + handrail extensions |

### 3.6 ADA accessibility (ICC A117.1 ┬¦504-505 + ADA 2010)

- **Handrail top extension**: 305 mm (12") oltre l'ultimo nosing del top landing, orizzontale.
- **Handrail bottom extension** (post-2010 ADA): = 1 tread depth oltre l'ultimo nosing (NON pi├╣ 305 mm fisso).
- **Contrast nosing strip**: 51 mm (2") leading edge contrasto visivo (ICC A117.1 ┬¦504.5).
- **Step variation**: Ōēż4.8 mm (3/16").
- **Validator** in Nestor: profilo `'ada'` opzionale.

### 3.7 Fire egress / occupancy load (IBC 2021 ch.10 + NFPA 101)

- Capacit├Ā: **0.3 inch/persona** sulle scale (formula `persone_max = larghezza_mm / 7.62`).
- 2 uscite obbligatorie se >49 persone OPPURE percorso comune >30m.
- Travel distance max: 75m (sprinklerizzato), 60m (non).
- **Scope Nestor**: warning su `width` insufficiente per `occupancyLoad` dichiarato. Travel distance OUT-OF-SCOPE (richiede grafo path-of-travel).

### 3.8 Cut line plane convention (ISO/DIN/ANSI standard)

- **Cut plane height**: standard architettonico **1.2m (4 ft)** sopra il pavimento.
- **Treads sotto cut plane**: linee SOLID continue.
- **Treads sopra cut plane**: linee DASHED tratteggiate (visibility hidden).
- **Break symbol**: zigzag/spezzata 45┬░ perpendicolare alla direzione di marcia (ISO 128).
- **Default Nestor**: `cutPlaneHeight = 1200 mm`, configurabile per-stair + project-default.

### 3.9 Out-of-scope industry-wide (documentazione esplicita, non gap Nestor)

Nessun major CAD (2026 SOTA) implementa nativamente:
- **Real-time anti-clash during draw** con muri/colonne (tutti usano batch Interference Check post-creazione: ArchiCAD Collision Detection AC21+, Revit Interference Check).
- **Cross-entity shared landings** (workaround universale = slab/floor entity separata).
- **Auto-generation della VIEW di sezione** (la vista ├© creata dall'utente; solo il plan-view cut split ├© automatico).

Nestor adotta lo stesso scope:  Phase 1-8 = no real-time clash, no cross-entity landings, no auto section view. Phase 9+ = extension point `stair-clash-checker`.

### 3.6 Modelli dati industry ŌĆö Associative vs Sketched

- **Component-based / Associative** (Revit, BricsCAD BIM, AutoCAD Architecture, Allplan): params ŌåÆ ricalcolo geometria. Editing parametrico, QTO strutturato.
- **Sketch-based** (Revit legacy, Vectorworks Vertex): user disegna walkline ŌåÆ tool deriva. Massima libert├Ā.

**Convergenza 2026**: Component-based standard moderno (Revit ha deprecato Sketch). Nestor adotta **Associative-first** + **Sketch** come tipologia.

### 3.7 Sub-elementi di una scala (decomposizione standard)

1. **Flight** (Žü╬¼╬ĮŽä╬┐/Žā╬║╬Ł╬╗╬┐Žé) 2. **Landing** (ŽĆ╬╗╬▒ŽäŽŹŽā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐) 3. **Tread** (ŽĆ╬¼Žä╬Ę╬╝╬▒+nosing) 4. **Riser** (Žü╬╣ŽćŽä╬»)
5. **Stringer** (╬╗╬»╬╝╬▒) 6. **Handrail** (╬║╬┐ŽģŽĆ╬▒ŽāŽä╬«) 7. **Baluster/Newel** (╬║╬¼╬│╬║╬Ą╬╗╬▒) 8. **Walkline** (╬│Žü╬▒╬╝╬╝╬« ŽĆ╬┐Žü╬Ą╬»╬▒Žé)

In 2D si rappresentano: contorno gradini, walkline tratteggiata, freccia + label UP/DOWN + n. gradini, linea di taglio se mezzo-piano.

---

## 4. Gap Analysis Google-Level

### G1 ŌĆö StairEntity nel discriminated union

`src/subapps/dxf-viewer/types/entities.ts` non contiene `'stair'`. Aggiungere `StairEntity` come **parametric entity** seguendo pattern ArrayEntity (`kind` + `params` + `geometry` cached).

### G2 ŌĆö Helper geometrici nuovi

| Helper | File da creare | Funzione |
|---|---|---|
| `spiralPointAt(t, params)` + `spiralArcLength` | `rendering/entities/shared/geometry-spiral-utils.ts` | Spirale archimedea/log + lunghezza Gauss-Legendre 10pt |
| `helixSample(t, params)` | `geometry-helix-utils.ts` | Punto 3D su elica |
| `ellipseArcLengthRamanujan(a,b)` + `ellipseSampleByArcLength` | extend `geometry-rendering-utils.ts` | Approx Ramanujan + sampling |
| `offsetPolyline(poly, distance)` | `geometry-offset-utils.ts` | Polyline parallela (stringers) |

### G3 ŌĆö Walkline + tread placement

- `computeWalkline(centerline, offset)`
- `placeTreadsAlongWalkline(walkline, stepCount)` ŌĆö riusa `samplePath` esistente da `path-arc-length-sampler.ts` Ō£ģ

### G4 ŌĆö Validator NOK + IBC + Eurocode

Estensione di `src/services/building-code/` (ADR-186):
- `src/services/building-code/engines/gate-stair-checker.ts` ŌĆö input `StairParams`, output `ValidationResult[]` con level `'hard-error' \| 'warning' \| 'ok'` + messageKey i18n.
- **Hard errors** (geom impossibili) bloccano creazione; **warnings** (code violation) lasciano passare ma marcano `validation.hasCodeViolations`.

### G5 ŌĆö Property panel post-creazione

Doppio livello:
1. **Contextual ribbon tab** "╬Ż╬║╬¼╬╗╬▒" (mirror ADR-344 Text contextual) ŌĆö param-base sempre visibili: kind, rise, tread, stepCount, width, codeProfile, validator badge.
2. **Floating Advanced Properties panel** apribile da bottone ŌĆö param avanzati: nosing, walklineOffset, handrails, materials placeholder (3D-ready), landings detail, winderMethod, validation report. Position persistente `dxf:stair.advancedPanel.{x,y,docked}`.

### G6 ŌĆö Enterprise ID + Firestore schema

- `STAIR: 'stair'` in `enterprise-id-prefixes.ts` ŌåÆ `generateStairId()`.
- **Nuova collection `floorplan_stairs`** (industry-aligned, Revit/ArchiCAD/AutoCAD Architecture/BricsCAD BIM + IFC 4 `IfcStair`).
- **Path: top-level `floorplan_stairs/{stairId}`** con tenant isolation via `companyId` field (Phase 8 2026-05-17 ŌĆö was sub-path `companies/{cid}/projects/{pid}/floorplan_stairs/{stairId}` in Phase 1 plan, switched to top-level to reuse `firestoreQueryService.subscribe` SSoT ŌĆö ADR-355 ŌĆö and inherit its ADR-361 equality guard upstream. Subscribe filters by `(projectId, floorplanId)`; tenant `companyId` filter applied auto by the service). Pattern mirrors `building_floorplans` / `project_floorplans`.
- Schema `StairDoc` = params + bbox cached + validation summary + optional `geometry`. Geometry recomputed client-side from params (ADR ┬¦G6) ŌĆö re-derivable, not load-bearing.
- Indici composite: `(companyId, projectId, floorplanId)` (subscribe primary), `(projectId, floorId, params.codeProfile)`, `(projectId, validation.hasCodeViolations, updatedAt)`.

### G7 ŌĆö 3D-readiness

Tutti i `Point2D` del modello stair sono `Point3D` con `z` opzionale. Renderer 2D ignora z; quando arriver├Ā 3D la struttura ├© gi├Ā pronta.

### G8 ŌĆö i18n stair namespace

`tools.stair.*` in `el/` + `en/` (name, description, steps, shortcuts, types, validation messages, panel labels, arrow.up/down).

### G9 ŌĆö Ribbon entry

Split-button "╬Ż╬║╬¼╬╗╬▒" in `home-tab-draw.ts` con 10 varianti live dal merge (no comingSoon): `straight, l-shape, u-shape, gamma, spiral, helical, elliptical, winder, triangular-fan, triangular-outline, sketch`.

### G11 ŌĆö Multi-storey: totalRise auto-derivato

`totalRise` oggi raw param. Industry (Revit Multistory, ArchiCAD Multi-Level): `totalRise` = `storyHeight ├Ś storyCount` da config livelli. Aggiungere `multiStoryConfig?: { topLevel: string; storyHeight: number; storyCount: number }` opzionale; quando presente, `totalRise` diventa COMPUTED; quando assente, raw input come oggi.

### G12 ŌĆö Stair structure type

Nessun campo `structureType`. Industry (ArchiCAD Structure branch, Allplan Stringer/Carriage tabs, Tekla S71/S82, Revit system families): 8 tipi standard. Aggiungere `structureType: 'monolithic'|'stringer-1side'|'stringer-2side'|'central-stringer'|'cantilever'|'suspended'|'glass-tread'|'steel-grating'` + `stringerParams?: { width; height; sides }`.

### G13 ŌĆö Materials & finishes + riser open/closed

Solo `nosing: number`. Mancano: `riserType: 'closed'|'open'` (impatta render 2D: riser aperto = linea tratteggiata). `materials?: { tread?; riser?; stringer?; landing? }` (string ID material library). `antiskidNosing: boolean`. `adaContrastStrip: boolean`. ArchiCAD pattern: per-stair default + per-tread override in Edit Mode.

### G14 ŌĆö Cut line render split

Oggi `cutLine?: Segment3D` ma nessuna logica di placement n├® split. Aggiungere: `cutPlaneHeight: number` (default 1200mm) in StairParams. `StairGeometry.treadsAboveCut: Polygon3D[]` + `treadsBelowCut: Polygon3D[]`. Render: sopra=dashed, sotto=solid. Break symbol zigzag 45┬░ auto-generato.

### G15 ŌĆö Edit grips post-creazione

Nessun sistema grip stair-specific. Industry (Revit direct manipulation, BricsCAD yellow/green grips, ArchiCAD pet palette, VisualARQ control points): `StairGripType = 'basePoint'|'directionGrip'|'widthGrip'|'lengthGrip'|'splitGrip'`. Pattern simile a line tool ADR-357.

### G16 ŌĆö Auto landing depth + corner style

`landingDepth` oggi `number` fisso. Industry: `'auto'` = `width`. Aggiungere: `landingDepth: 'auto'|number`, `landingCornerStyle?: 'square'|'chamfer'|'fillet'`, `landingCornerRadius?: number`.

### G17 ŌĆö Mirror/rotate/copy semantica

Mirror su scala parametrica DEVE invertire `turnDirection` (cwŌåöccw) e `turnSequence` (leftŌåöright). Lasciare al renderer = rottura editabilit├Ā (Revit bug noto). Helper `mirrorStairParams(params, axis)` + `rotateStairParams(params, angle, pivot)` + `copyStairParams(params, offset)` come SSoT.

### G18 ŌĆö Code profiles aggiuntivi

`codeProfile` esteso a `'nok'|'ibc'|'eurocode'|'nbc'|'nfpa'|'as1657'|'din'|'ada'|'none'`. Default `'nok'`.

### G19 ŌĆö ADA handrail extensions

`handrails` esteso: `topExtension?: number` (default 305mm), `bottomExtension?: 'one-tread'|number`. Profilo `'ada'` valida.

### G20 ŌĆö Egress capacity validator

Campo `occupancyLoad?: number` opzionale per-stair (o ereditato per-progetto via setting). Validator warning se `width < occupancyLoad ├Ś 7.62`. Travel distance OUT-OF-SCOPE.

### G21 ŌĆö Tread numbering & labels

Mancano. Aggiungere: `treadNumberStart: number` (default 1), `treadLabelDisplay: 'all'|'nth'|'none'` (default `'none'` plan-view + `'all'` schedule-export), `treadLabelEveryN?: number` (per `'nth'`), `treadLabelRestartPerFlight: boolean` (default true).

### G22 ŌĆö Headroom check (clash con elementi sopra)

Validator estensione: `headroomClear` calcolato confrontando bbox stair+walkline con `floorplan_walls`/`floorplan_columns`/`ceiling_slab` overhead. Real-time durante draw = raro industry (Revit batch post-creation ├© lo standard). Default: post-creation warning, non-bloccante.

### G23 ŌĆö QTO + Schedule export

IFC4 `Qto_StairBaseQuantities`: `GrossVolume`, `NetVolume`, `GrossFootprintArea`, `NetSideArea`, `Height`, `Length`. Schedule export CSV/Excel/PDF. Nuovo SSoT: `stair-schedule-exporter`.

### G24 ŌĆö Audit trail + soft-lock multi-user

`EntityAuditService.recordChange()` (ADR-195) copre gi├Ā history. **Wired 2026-05-27 via ADR-380**: `recordStairChange()` thin client (`bim/stairs/stair-audit-client.ts`) + `STAIR_TRACKED_FIELDS` registry (~28 fields) + `use-stair-persistence.ts` capture prevParams + full snapshot on delete. Soft-lock display-only: `editingBy?: { userId: string; since: Timestamp }` in StairDoc. Non-bloccante (non lock vero, solo indicator UI). CRDT full = Phase 9+.

### G25 ŌĆö Hotkey shortcut

Convenzione: `'st'` (Stair) ŌĆö Revit-aligned (SR ridotto a ST), 2 lettere, no conflict con `L` (line). In `TOOL_DEFINITIONS['stair']`.

### G26 ŌĆö Library presets

`StairPreset: { id; name; params: Partial<StairParams>; kind; scope: 'user'|'company'|'project' }`. Firestore: `companies/{cid}/stair_presets/{presetId}`. UI: "Save as preset" + dropdown "Load preset" in contextual ribbon. Nuovo SSoT: `stair-presets-service`.

### G27-G33 ŌĆö Out-of-scope o Phase 9+ (documentati, non gap)

| G | Tema | Ragione |
|---|------|---------|
| G27 | Stair-to-stair shared landings cross-entity | Industry-wide non implementato. Workaround Rectangle entity. Phase 9+ `sharedLandingRef?` |
| G28 | Custom step profile (poligono libero) | Phase 1-8: solo `nosingSide: 'front'\|'none'\|'front-and-sides'` enum. Custom polygon Phase 9 |
| G29 | Real-time CRDT collaboration | Over-engineering Phase 1-8. G24 soft-lock copre il caso |
| G30 | Anti-clash real-time during draw | Industry SOTA = batch post-creation. Phase 9+ extension point `stair-clash-checker` |
| G31 | Glass railing 3D detail (LOD 300/350/400) | Phase 9 (3D renderer) |
| G32 | Performance >100 stairs | Gi├Ā coperto da ADR-040 micro-leaf + bitmap cache architecture |
| G33 | Auto-generation VIEW di sezione | Industry-wide non automatico (solo plan-cut split = G14). Out-of-scope |

---

## 5. Decision

### 5.0 Sistema di unit├Ā

- **Storage canonico**: mm interno + Firestore + DXF export (ISO).
- **Display utente**: switchabile cm/mm via setting `dxf:units.stair` (localStorage SSoT).
- **Default**: `cm` (mercato GR).
- **Formatter SSoT**: `formatStairLength(mmValue, unit)` in `systems/stairs/stair-units.ts`.
- **Parser SSoT**: `parseStairLength(text)` accetta "17.5 cm" / "175 mm" / "17,5".
- Tutti i Dynamic Input + Property Panel + Ribbon Properties usano lo stesso formatter/parser.

### 5.1 Modello dati ŌĆö **Associative Parametric**

```typescript
// types/stair.ts (NEW)
export type StairKind =
  | 'straight'
  | 'l-shape'             // ┬╝ turn (90┬░)
  | 'u-shape'             // ┬Į turn (180┬░), mid-landing
  | 'gamma'               // 3 flights + 2 landings (╬ō shape)
  | 'spiral'              // archimedean, no inner radius
  | 'helical'             // open-well circular, inner radius > 0
  | 'elliptical'          // elliptical helical
  | 'winder'              // straight + winder treads at corner
                          //   method 'kite' = 3 treads in 90┬░, middle triangular
  | 'triangular-fan'      // ╬▓╬Ą╬ĮŽä╬¼╬╗╬╣╬▒: uniform angular treads ŌåÆ apex (polygonal spiral)
  | 'triangular-outline'  // wedge layout fitting triangular room footprint
  | 'sketch';             // user-drawn walkline ŌåÆ derived geometry

export interface StairParams {
  basePoint: Point3D;
  direction: number;        // deg, 0 = +X

  rise: number;             // mm
  tread: number;            // mm (excl. nosing)
  nosing: number;           // mm
  nosingSide: 'front' | 'none' | 'front-and-sides';   // G28
  width: number;            // mm
  stepCount: number;

  totalRise: number;        // raw OR computed da multiStoryConfig (G11)
  totalRun: number;
  pitch: number;            // deg

  multiStoryConfig?: {                                  // G11
    topLevel: string;
    storyHeight: number;    // mm
    storyCount: number;
  };

  structureType:                                        // G12
    | 'monolithic'
    | 'stringer-1side'
    | 'stringer-2side'
    | 'central-stringer'
    | 'cantilever'
    | 'suspended'
    | 'glass-tread'
    | 'steel-grating';
  stringerParams?: {                                    // G12
    width: number;          // mm
    height: number;         // mm
    sides: 'left' | 'right' | 'both' | 'center';
  };

  riserType: 'closed' | 'open';                         // G13
  materials?: {                                         // G13
    tread?: string;         // material library ID
    riser?: string;
    stringer?: string;
    landing?: string;
  };
  perTreadOverrides?: Record<number, Partial<{          // G13 ArchiCAD pattern
    material: string;
    nosing: number;
    customProfile?: Point2D[];
  }>>;
  antiskidNosing: boolean;                              // G13
  adaContrastStrip: boolean;                            // G13/G19

  cutPlaneHeight: number;                               // G14, default 1200 mm

  variant: StairVariantParams;

  walklineOffset: number;   // mm (default 300)
  handrails: {
    inner: boolean;
    outer: boolean;
    height: number;         // mm (default 900)
    topExtension?: number;  // mm (G19, ADA default 305)
    bottomExtension?: 'one-tread' | number;             // G19
  };
  upDirection: 'forward' | 'backward';

  treadNumberStart: number;                             // G21 default 1
  treadLabelDisplay: 'all' | 'nth' | 'none';            // G21
  treadLabelEveryN?: number;                            // G21
  treadLabelRestartPerFlight: boolean;                  // G21

  occupancyLoad?: number;                               // G20

  codeProfile:                                          // G18 esteso
    | 'nok' | 'ibc' | 'eurocode'
    | 'nbc' | 'nfpa' | 'as1657' | 'din' | 'ada' | 'none';
  nokSubType?: 'main' | 'secondary';   // toggle in panel quando codeProfile='nok'
}

export type StairVariantParams =
  | { kind: 'straight' }
  | { kind: 'l-shape'; turnDirection: 'left'|'right'; landingDepth: 'auto'|number; landingCornerStyle?: 'square'|'chamfer'|'fillet'; landingCornerRadius?: number; flightSplit: [number, number]; }
  | { kind: 'u-shape'; turnDirection: 'left'|'right'; landingDepth: 'auto'|number; landingCornerStyle?: 'square'|'chamfer'|'fillet'; landingCornerRadius?: number; flightSplit: [number, number]; }
  | { kind: 'gamma'; turnSequence: ['left'|'right', 'left'|'right']; landings: ['auto'|number, 'auto'|number]; landingCornerStyle?: 'square'|'chamfer'|'fillet'; flightSplit: [number, number, number]; }
  | { kind: 'spiral'; centerPoint: Point3D; innerRadius: 0; sweepAngle: number; turnDirection: 'cw'|'ccw'; }
  | { kind: 'helical'; centerPoint: Point3D; innerRadius: number; outerRadius: number; sweepAngle: number; turnDirection: 'cw'|'ccw'; }
    // panel mostra 3 campi sincronizzati (innerRadius/width/outerRadius), 1 derivato (constraint outer = inner + width).
  | { kind: 'elliptical'; centerPoint: Point3D; semiMajor: number; semiMinor: number; sweepAngle: number; turnDirection: 'cw'|'ccw'; rotation: number; }
  | { kind: 'winder'; turnAngle: number; winderCount: number; winderMethod: 'equal-going'|'kite'|'balanced'|'pie'; }
  | { kind: 'triangular-fan'; apexPoint: Point3D; openingAngle: number; stepCountPerArc: number; turnDirection: 'cw'|'ccw'; }
  | { kind: 'triangular-outline'; triangleVertices: [Point3D, Point3D, Point3D]; entrySide: 0|1|2; orientation: 'cw'|'ccw'; }
  | { kind: 'sketch'; walklinePath: Point3D[]; };

export interface StairGeometry {
  treads: Polygon3D[];                      // legacy alias = treadsBelowCut
  treadsBelowCut: Polygon3D[];              // G14 ŌĆö solid render
  treadsAboveCut: Polygon3D[];              // G14 ŌĆö dashed render
  risers: Segment3D[];
  stringers: { inner: Polyline3D; outer: Polyline3D; };
  walkline: Polyline3D;
  handrails: { inner?: Polyline3D; outer?: Polyline3D; };
  landings: Polygon3D[];
  arrowSymbol: { start: Point3D; end: Point3D; label: 'UP'|'DOWN'; };
  cutLine?: Segment3D;                      // break symbol zigzag 45┬░ (G14)
  treadLabels?: { treadIndex: number; position: Point3D; text: string; }[];   // G21
  bbox: BoundingBox3D;
}

export interface StairEntity extends BaseEntity {
  type: 'stair';
  kind: StairKind;
  params: StairParams;
  geometry: StairGeometry;        // computed cache
  validation: {
    hasCodeViolations: boolean;
    violationKeys: string[];      // i18n message keys
    headroomViolations?: string[];                            // G22
    egressViolations?: string[];                              // G20
    adaViolations?: string[];                                 // G19
    lastValidatedAt: Timestamp;
  };
  editingBy?: { userId: string; since: Timestamp };           // G24 soft-lock display-only
  qto?: {                                                     // G23 IFC4 Qto_StairBaseQuantities
    grossVolume: number;          // m┬│
    netVolume: number;            // m┬│
    grossFootprintArea: number;   // m┬▓
    netSideArea: number;          // m┬▓
    height: number;               // mm
    length: number;               // mm
    handrailLinearMeters: number; // m
    treadCladdingArea: number;    // m┬▓
  };
}
```

### 5.2 Pipeline tool ŌĆö Modalit├Ā **Ibrida**

```
Ribbon click "╬Ż╬║╬¼╬╗╬▒" ŌåÆ ToolStateStore.setTool('stair')
  Ō¢╝
StairContextualPanel mounts in ribbon (sticky, NOT modal):
  - Type selector (split: 10 kinds)
  - Always-visible params: rise ┬Ę tread ┬Ę stepCount ┬Ę width
  - Collapsible "MoreŌĆ”": nosing, walklineOffset, handrails, landings, codeProfile
  - Live validator badge (NOK/IBC) ŌĆö verde/giallo/rosso
  Ō¢╝
DrawingStateMachine: IDLE ŌåÆ TOOL_READY
  Ō¢╝
[Click 1] basePoint (anchor low end)
[Mouse move] preview ruota+riposiziona seguendo cursore
[Click 2] direction (orientation) ŌĆö OR Dynamic Input for absolute angle
  Ō¢╝
COLLECTING_POINTS ŌĆö params editabili live dal ribbon panel:
  ogni cambio param ŌåÆ ricalcolo preview real-time (riusa PreviewCanvas ADR-040)
  Ō¢╝
[Enter / OK / Right-clickŌåÆFinish] ŌåÆ completeEntity(StairEntity)
  ŌåÆ CreateEntityCommand ŌåÆ CommandHistory (undo/redo)
  ŌåÆ SceneManager.addEntity
  ŌåÆ Firestore persistence (collection floorplan_stairs)
  Ō¢╝
Tool resta attivo (continuous mode); ESC esce a 'select'.
```

Panel persiste cross-session in `dxf:stair.lastParams` (localStorage).

### 5.3 Sub-elementi (SSoT mapping)

| Sub-element | Riusa | Nuovo helper |
|---|---|---|
| Treads | `Polygon3D` + drawPath | `computeTreadGeometry(params)` |
| Risers | `Segment3D` | derived from treads |
| Stringers | `Polyline3D` + `offsetPolyline` | NEW `geometry-offset-utils.ts` |
| Walkline | `Polyline3D` + `samplePath` (existing) | `computeWalkline(centerline, offset)` |
| Spiral/Helical/Elliptical | NEW helpers (G2) | spiral, helix, ellipseSample |
| Handrails | `Polyline3D` | `computeHandrail(walkline, height)` |
| Validator | ADR-186 engine | `gate-stair-checker.ts` |

### 5.4 Nuovi SSoT da creare (count = 8, round 2)

1. **`StairGeometryService`** ŌĆö `systems/stairs/StairGeometryService.ts` ŌĆö entry point `computeStairGeometry(params): StairGeometry`, dispatch per kind.
2. **`stair-validator`** ŌĆö `systems/stairs/stair-validator.ts` ŌĆö `validateStairParams(params, codeProfile, contextEntities?): ValidationResult[]`. Estesa con headroom (G22), egress (G20), ADA (G19).
3. **`geometry-offset-utils`** ŌĆö `rendering/entities/shared/geometry-offset-utils.ts` ŌĆö `offsetPolyline(poly, distance)`.
4. **`geometry-curve-utils`** ŌĆö spiral + helix + ellipse arc-length sampling (raggruppati).
5. **`stair-grips`** ŌĆö `systems/stairs/stair-grips.ts` ŌĆö G15 ŌĆö `getStairGrips(entity): StairGrip[]` + handler `applyGripDrag(entity, gripType, delta): StairParams`. 5 tipi: basePoint/direction/width/length/split.
6. **`stair-transforms`** ŌĆö `systems/stairs/stair-transforms.ts` ŌĆö G17 ŌĆö `mirrorStairParams(params, axis)` + `rotateStairParams(params, angle, pivot)` + `copyStairParams(params, offset)`. Inverte semanticamente turnDirection/turnSequence.
7. **`stair-presets-service`** ŌĆö `systems/stairs/stair-presets-service.ts` ŌĆö G26 ŌĆö CRUD su `companies/{cid}/stair_presets/{presetId}`, scope user/company/project, cache 5min.
8. **`stair-schedule-exporter`** ŌĆö `systems/stairs/stair-schedule-exporter.ts` ŌĆö G23 ŌĆö produce CSV/Excel/PDF da array `StairEntity` con `Qto_StairBaseQuantities`.

### 5.5 Nuovi flag `TOOL_DEFINITIONS`

```typescript
'stair': {
  category: 'drawing',
  requiresCanvas: true,
  canInterrupt: true,
  allowsContinuous: false,
  allowsChain: false,
  supportsDynamicInput: true,
  preservesOverlayMode: false,
  hotkey: 'st',                     // G25 Revit-aligned (SR ridotto)
}
```

### 5.6 Enterprise ID

`STAIR: 'stair'` ŌåÆ `generateStairId()` ŌåÆ IDs `stair_<ulid26>`.

### 5.7 Walkline visibility (industry-aligned)

ORATA durante draw/edit mode, NASCOSTA dopo finalization (default). Toggle "╬Ģ╬╝Žå╬¼╬Į╬╣Žā╬Ę ╬│Žü╬▒╬╝╬╝╬«Žé ŽĆ╬┐Žü╬Ą╬»╬▒Žé" in panel per export documentazione ╬Ø╬¤╬Ü. Convergenza AutoCAD/Revit/ArchiCAD/Vectorworks/IFC.

### 5.8 Arrow label format

i18n locale-driven. Chiave `tools.stair.arrow.up/down` + counter `{count} ╬▓╬▒╬Ė╬╝╬»╬┤╬ĄŽé/risers`. Format SSoT `stair-label-formatter.ts`.
- EL: "╬æ╬Ø╬® 16 ╬▓╬▒╬Ė╬╝╬»╬┤╬ĄŽé" / "╬Ü╬æ╬ż╬® 16 ╬▓╬▒╬Ė╬╝╬»╬┤╬ĄŽé"
- EN: "UP 16 risers" / "DOWN 16 risers"

### 5.9 Validator behavior (hybrid)

- **Hard errors** (geometricamente impossibili): `stepCount<=0`, `width<=0`, `rise<=0`, `tread<=0`, area negativa, self-intersection ŌåÆ **BLOCCANO** creazione.
- **Code violations** (NOK/IBC out-of-range) ŌåÆ **WARN** non-bloccante, badge rosso in panel + tooltip lista violazioni; entity creata ma marcata `validation.hasCodeViolations=true` per audit.

### 5.10 NOK subtype

Toggle `╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒/╬┤╬ĄŽģŽä╬ĄŽü╬ĄŽŹ╬┐ŽģŽā╬▒` in panel quando `codeProfile='nok'`. Default `╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒`. Validator switcha range dinamicamente.
- Defaults ╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒: W=1200, R=175, G=280.
- Defaults ╬┤╬ĄŽģŽä╬ĄŽü╬ĄŽŹ╬┐ŽģŽā╬▒: W=900, R=180, G=270.

### 5.11 Transform operations (G17)

Mirror/rotate/copy NON sono operazioni geometriche raw ŌĆö devono trasformare semanticamente i `params`.

```typescript
// systems/stairs/stair-transforms.ts
export function mirrorStairParams(params: StairParams, axis: Line2D): StairParams {
  // 1. mirror basePoint geometricamente
  // 2. INVERTE turnDirection (cwŌåöccw, leftŌåöright) nel variant
  // 3. INVERTE turnSequence array per kind='gamma'
  // 4. Se nosingSide='front-and-sides' resta uguale; 'front' resta 'front'
}
export function rotateStairParams(params: StairParams, angle: number, pivot: Point3D): StairParams {
  // ruota basePoint + direction; variant resta invariato
}
export function copyStairParams(params: StairParams, offset: Point3D): StairParams {
  // sposta basePoint, tutto il resto invariato
}
```

Render di una mirrored/rotated stair = `computeStairGeometry(transformedParams)`. Editabilit├Ā preservata (Revit bug noto evitato).

### 5.12 Stair Grips system (G15)

> ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ **SUPERSEDED da [ADR-393](./ADR-393-bim-stair-extended-grips.md) (2026-05-28).** Il set originale di 5 grip qui sotto ├© stato esteso a 13: aggiunti 4 corner asimmetrici (straight) + mid-front start + 2 per-flight landing-edge + landing depth/corner-radius (L/U/╬ō). Il `splitGrip` (centroid) ├© stato **rimosso** e sostituito dai due grip sui bordi del landing (`stair-flight1-end` / `stair-flight2-start`). Implementazione: `bim/stairs/stair-grips.ts` (posizioni) + `stair-grip-transforms.ts` (drag) + `stair-grip-math.ts` (helper, consuma `stair-geometry-shared`). Questa tabella resta come riferimento storico dei 4 grip base ancora attivi (`stair-base`/`stair-direction`/`stair-width`/`stair-length`).

Post-creazione, selezionando una stair, appaiono i grip overlay (4 base + ADR-393):

| Grip | Posizione | Drag effect |
|------|-----------|-------------|
| `basePoint` | basePoint | sposta tutto (no recalc geometry, solo translate) |
| `directionGrip` | basePoint + direction ├Ś 100mm (scene-scaled, ADR-393 ┬¦8.1) | ruota direction (no width/stepCount change) |
| `widthGrip` | midpoint outer stringer | cambia `width` (recalc geometry, walkline shifts) |
| `lengthGrip` | end di ultimo step | cambia `stepCount` derivando da nuova length / tread |
| ~~`splitGrip`~~ | ~~midpoint landing~~ | **rimosso in ADR-393** ŌåÆ `stair-flight1-end` + `stair-flight2-start` |

Implementati come overlay layer riusando architettura grip esistente del line tool (ADR-357). Snap+ortho+polar funzionano durante drag.

---

## 6. Architecture

### 6.1 Layered diagram

```
ŌöīŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöÉ

Ōöé  ŌöīŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöÉ  ŌöīŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöÉ                    Ōöé
Ōöé  Ōöé ToolStateStore   Ōöé  Ōöé useStairTool (hook)    Ōöé                    Ōöé
Ōöé  Ōöé activeTool=stair Ōöé  Ōöé COLLECTING_POINTS state Ōöé                    Ōöé
Ōöé  ŌööŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌö¼ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöś  ŌööŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌö¼ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöś                    Ōöé
```

### 6.2 Render pipeline (2D plan view) ŌĆö round 2 con cut split (G14)

Decomposizione `StairEntity` per render:
1. Per ogni tread in `geometry.treadsBelowCut` (sotto cut plane 1.2m): drawPolygon SOLID (fill = layer color, stroke continuous).
2. Per ogni tread in `geometry.treadsAboveCut`: drawPolygon DASHED (stroke tratteggiato, hidden).
3. Per ogni `riser` in `geometry.risers`: drawLine; if `params.riserType='open'` ŌåÆ DASHED, else SOLID. **Convention (ADR-370 Phase 5.3, 2026-05-25)**: `Segment3D` per riser ├© encoded DIAGONALMENTE ŌĆö `start` = corner A @zLow su un width edge, `end` = corner B OPPOSTO @zHigh sull'altro edge. Il 2D `drawLine(start.xy, end.xy)` produce direttamente la linea di footprint del riser nel plan view; il 3D `StairToThreeConverter.buildRiserBox` deriva midpoint + width axis + width magnitude dal diagonale (no extra context). Convention sostituisce il legacy "vertical line at one edge" (start.xy === end.xy) che era unimplemented in 2D e silently broken in 3D.
4. `walkline`: drawPolyline dashed (visibile solo se editing OR toggle ON, ADR ┬¦5.7).
5. `arrowSymbol`: drawArrow + drawText (i18n locale-driven).
6. **Plan symbology per `structureType`** (Phase 7c, 2026-05-25 ŌĆö `stair-render-structure-style.ts`): treads + stringers vengono differenziati al render-boundary in base a `params.structureType`. Mapping industry-standard (Revit / ArchiCAD / AutoCAD Arch convergence):
   - `monolithic` ŌåÆ treads solid fill, **no stringer line** (mass concrete reads dall'outline).
   - `stringer-1side` ŌåÆ treads solid + **outer stringer only**, bold.
   - `stringer-2side` ŌåÆ treads solid + **both stringers** bold (legacy default).
   - `central-stringer` ŌåÆ treads solid + **walkline** (= geometric centerline tra inner/outer) bold.
   - `cantilever` ŌåÆ treads solid + **inner stringer only** (wall mount edge), bold.
   - `suspended` ŌåÆ treads solid + **both stringers dashed thin** (cable indication).
   - `glass-tread` ŌåÆ treads con dashed outline + fill ultra-light (`╬▒=0.04`) + stringers normali (frame metallico).
   - `steel-grating` ŌåÆ treads solid + **45┬░ hatch fill** (ISO 128 / ASME Y14.2 grating symbol) + stringers normali.
   La geometria (`geometry.stringers.inner/outer/walkline`) resta SSoT invariato ŌĆö solo il renderer sceglie quali polilinee usare per quale stile.
7. Handrails: drawPolyline tratteggiata (simbolico 2D). Top/bottom extension (G19) renderizzate se profile='ada'.
8. `cutLine`: linea spezzata 45┬░ zigzag (ISO 128) perpendicolare alla direzione di marcia.
9. `treadLabels` (G21): drawText su ogni tread o ogni N (default `display='none'` plan-view, `'all'` schedule-export).
10. ADA contrast strip nosing: linea bold colore contrasto sul leading edge se `adaContrastStrip=true`.

### 6.3 3D-readiness (Phase 9+)

- `Polygon3D` ŌåÆ extrude tread thickness.
- `Riser` ŌåÆ quad verticale altezza `rise`. **Phase 5.3 (2026-05-25)**: `StairToThreeConverter.buildRiserBox` consuma `Segment3D` diagonal encoding (start/end su corner opposti) ŌĆö `BoxGeometry(thicknessM, riseM, widthM)` con `widthM = |end.xy ŌłÆ start.xy|`, posizione = midpoint, `mesh.rotation.y = atan2(dxScene, -dyScene)`. Indipendente da `params.direction` (funziona uniformemente per straight/curved/winder kinds).
- Stringer ŌåÆ extruded beam.
- Handrail ŌåÆ swept profile lungo walkline traslata di `handrailHeight` in z.
- Spiral/Helical: `helixSample` ritorna gi├Ā `Point3D` con z calcolato.

Tutto il modello ├© 3D-ready oggi. Phase 9 aggiunge solo il renderer, zero refactor dati.

### 6.4 IFC export readiness (Phase 9+)

`floorplan_stairs.{stairId}` ŌåÆ `IfcStair` 1:1 (IFC 4.3.2):
- `IfcStair` aggrega `IfcStairFlight[]` (rampe) + `IfcSlab[PredefinedType=LANDING]` (pianerottoli).
- `IfcStair.PredefinedType` (`IfcStairTypeEnum`) mapping da `kind`:
  - `straight` ŌåÆ `STRAIGHT_RUN_STAIR`
  - `l-shape` ŌåÆ `QUARTER_TURN_STAIR`
  - `u-shape` ŌåÆ `HALF_TURN_STAIR`
  - `gamma` ŌåÆ `THREE_QUARTER_TURN_STAIR`
  - `spiral` ŌåÆ `SPIRAL_STAIR`
  - `helical` ŌåÆ `CURVED_RUN_STAIR`
  - `elliptical` ŌåÆ `CURVED_RUN_STAIR` (con properties extra)
  - `winder` ŌåÆ `QUARTER_WINDING_STAIR` (o `HALF_WINDING_STAIR` se 180┬░)
  - `triangular-fan` / `triangular-outline` ŌåÆ `USERDEFINED`
  - `sketch` ŌåÆ `USERDEFINED`
- **Pset_StairCommon**: `Reference`, `NumberOfRiser`, `NumberOfTreads`, `RiserHeight`, `TreadLength`, `RequiredHeadroom`, `HandicapAccessible` (ŌåÉ `codeProfile='ada'`), `FireExit` (ŌåÉ `occupancyLoad>0`).
- **Qto_StairBaseQuantities** (G23): `GrossVolume`, `NetVolume`, `GrossFootprintArea`, `NetSideArea`, `Height`, `Length`.
- **IfcRailing** (G18 separate entity): `Pset_RailingCommon` con `IsExternal`, `Reference`, `FireRating`. PredefinedType: `HANDRAIL`/`GUARDRAIL`/`BALUSTRADE`.
- Rebar (Eurocode 2): `IfcReinforcingBar[]` come oggetti FIGLI di `IfcStairFlight` (Tekla pattern).

### 6.5 QTO + Schedule export (G23)

Pipeline: `stair-schedule-exporter.ts` accetta array `StairEntity[]` + format target (CSV/Excel/PDF).

```typescript
// Formato schedule row:
{
  stairId, kind, structureType,
  riserCount, riserHeight, treadDepth, totalRise, totalRun,
  slopeDeg, headroomClear, occupancyLoad,
  codeCompliance: { profile, hasViolations, violationCount },
  qto: { grossVolume, netVolume, grossFootprintArea, netSideArea, height, length, handrailLinearMeters }
}
```

Export CSV via `papaparse`. Excel via `xlsx`. PDF via `jspdf` riusando template existing.

### 6.6 Presets pipeline (G26)

```
"Save as preset" button ŌåÆ modal:
  - name (utente)
  - scope: 'user' | 'company' | 'project'
  - kind (auto-detected da current stair)
  Ō¢╝
StairPreset ŌåÆ Firestore companies/{cid}/stair_presets/{presetId}
  Ō¢╝
"Load preset" dropdown in contextual ribbon:
  - lista filtrata per (scope, kind, codeProfile)
  - applica params al tool corrente preservando basePoint/direction
```

ID via `enterprise-id.service.ts` prefix `STAIR_PRESET: 'sprst'`. Cache 5min client-side.

### 6.7 Headroom clash check pipeline (G22)

Trigger: post-creation OR on-edit (debounced 500ms).

```
1. computeStairGeometry(params) ŌåÆ walkline + bbox 3D.
2. Query SceneManager: entities sopra walkline (z > walkline.z + headroomClear).
3. Per ogni entity overhead (wall/column/slab/ceiling):
   - se bbox.z_bottom < walkline.z + headroomMin ŌåÆ violation.
4. Append violations a entity.validation.headroomViolations.
5. UI badge giallo nel contextual ribbon panel.
```

Real-time during draw ├© OPZIONALE (G22 default = post-creation). Industry standard.

### 6.7.1 Floor link bridge (Phase 9 Plan A, Q17)

Stair `multiStoryConfig.storyHeight` is bound to the building floor's `height` (m) when a `floorId` is in scope (`levelManager.saveContext.entityType === 'floor'`). Wiring:

```
useSpecialTools
  ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ useFloorMetadata(saveContext.floorId)        ŌåÉ Firestore subscribe (FLOORS/{id})
        ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ getFloorLink() : StairFloorLinkInput   ŌåÉ passed to useStairTool
              ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ buildDefaultStairParams(..., floorLink)
                    ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ multiStoryConfig = {
                          topLevel: floorId,
                          storyHeight: floor.height * 1000,
                          storyCount: 1,
                          linkedToFloor: true,
                        }

Ribbon contextual tab ŌåÆ RibbonStairFloorInfoWidget
  Ōö£ŌöĆŌöĆ reads FLOORS/{id} via useFloorMetadata (same SSoT subscription)
  Ōö£ŌöĆŌöĆ isLinkedToFloor(config, floor) tolerates legacy stairs missing the flag
  Ōöé   (Ōēż0.5mm tolerance match against `floor.height * 1000`)
  Ōö£ŌöĆŌöĆ badge ­¤öŚ (linked) or ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ (custom)
  ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ "Reset to floor" ŌåÆ UpdateStairParamsCommand sets linkedToFloor=true

Manual edits (ribbon storyHeight combobox, future grip drag, command patch)
  ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ useRibbonStairBridge.patchStoryHeight ŌåÆ linkedToFloor=false
```

Phase 9B-2 (strict mode, Q35) extends the bridge with `reconcileLinkedStair`
applied on every write path so a linked stair stays geometrically bound to
the floor envelope:

```
buildDefaultStairParams(..., floorLink)        ŌåÉ post-build reconcile
useRibbonStairBridge.patchRise                 ŌåÉ rise = primary lever
  ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ withRecomputedTotals ŌåÆ reconcileLinkedStair
        stepCount = round(storyHeight ├Ś storyCount / rise_mm)
        totalRise = storyHeight ├Ś storyCount   ŌåÉ LOCKED
useRibbonStairBridge.patchStepCount            ŌåÉ stepCount = secondary lever
  ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ deriveRiseFromStepCount(...) ŌåÆ withRecomputedTotals ŌåÆ reconcile
stair-grips.resizeLength (length grip)         ŌåÉ clamp + magnet snap
  ŌööŌöĆŌöĆ maxRun = tread ├Ś (maxStepCount ŌłÆ 1)
        if cursor in last 10% of maxRun ŌåÆ snap to maxRun
autoFixStairParams                             ŌåÉ reconcile FIRST, then code fix
stair-validator.checkStoryHeightOverflow       ŌåÉ hardError when linked (red)
stair-validator.checkStoryHeightUnderflow      ŌåÉ hardError when linked (red)
```

Phase 9B-3 hides the ribbon `storyHeight` combobox when linked
(`STAIR_RIBBON_VISIBILITY_KEYS.multiStoryHeightEditor`); the floor info widget
is then the sole surface that displays the height ŌĆö single source of truth.

Unit conventions: `FloorRecord.height` is stored in meters in the `FLOORS` collection; `StairMultiStoryConfig.storyHeight` is stored in millimeters (consistent with Phase 7a presets). The m ŌåÆ mm conversion happens at the bridge layer (auto-init builder + Reset button), never in the geometry pipeline.

Industry convergence: Revit Type Selector binds to Levels with explicit "Inherit" toggle; ArchiCAD Story Sensitive elements display "From Story X" label; AutoCAD Architecture stair elevation references a level marker. All three surface a visual link badge and a one-shot "restore link" affordance ŌĆö same UX adopted here. Strict-mode derivation (Phase 9B-2) follows the same 5/5 vendor convergence (Revit "Desired Riser Height" + ArchiCAD Story Sensitive Stair + AutoCAD Architecture `bindToLevels` + Vectorworks story snap + BricsCAD BIMSTAIR).

### 6.8 Multi-user soft-lock (G24, cita ADR-195)

`editingBy?: { userId; since }` settato ottimisticamente quando user inizia edit, cleared dopo `completeEntity` o timeout 5min. Display: badge "Editing by MariaŌĆ”" in contextual ribbon. NON blocca altri utenti (display-only). Audit completo via `EntityAuditService.recordChange()` (ADR-195) ŌĆö nessun nuovo sistema.

CRDT collaboration full = Phase 9+ se richiesto.

---

## 7. Implementation Phases (incremental, **1 sessione = 1 fase**, commit eseguito da Giorgio)

### 7.0 Commit & Push policy ŌĆö NON-NEGOTIABLE (2026-05-16)

**L'agente NON committa e NON pusha mai senza ordine esplicito di Giorgio.**

- L'agente esegue l'implementazione completa della Phase (codice + ADR update Phase 3) e poi **si ferma**.
- L'agente attende ordine esplicito ("commit" / "╬║╬¼╬Į╬Ą commit" / "commit it") prima di eseguire `git commit`.
- L'agente attende ordine esplicito ("push" / "ŽāŽä╬Ą╬»╬╗╬Ą" / "╬▒╬Į╬Ł╬▓╬▒Žā╬Ą" / "ŽĆ╬«╬│╬▒╬╣╬Į╬Ą Vercel") prima di eseguire `git push`.
- **Override globale**: CLAUDE.md SOS. N.(-1). Questa sezione lo riafferma a livello ADR per chiarezza operativa.
- **Why**: Giorgio decide cosa ├© production-ready. Ogni push = Vercel build = consumo crediti ($).

### 7.1 Context-budget rationale (2026-05-16)

Ogni fase deve completarsi in **una sola sessione Claude** con context Ōēż70% (target). Le fasi XL/L originali sono state splittate in sub-fasi per garantire context pulito ad ogni inizio. Classificazione:
- **S** (Ōēż3 file, Ōēż300 LOC): 1 sessione sicura
- **M** (4-6 file, ~400-800 LOC): 1 sessione OK
- **L** (5-8 file, ~800-1500 LOC): 1 sessione tight ma fattibile
- **XL** (>8 file, >1500 LOC): ŌØī vietato ŌåÆ split obbligatorio

### 7.2 Tabella fasi (post-split, 19 sessioni)

| **9B-2** Ō£ģ | Strict floor-bound stair mode (Q35). **Pre-merge gate per ogni Phase**:
- TypeScript zero errors
- SSoT ratchet zero new violations
- i18n ratchet zero new hardcoded
- Test coverage StairGeometryService Ōēź80% (presubmit grade)
- Visual regression baseline (ADR-343) aggiornato per ogni nuovo kind

---

## 8. Testing Strategy

- **Unit tests** (Jest) per ogni pure function:
  - `computeStairGeometry` per kind (10 input ŌåÆ expected geometry snapshot).
  - `validateStairParams` (matrix params ├Ś codeProfile).
  - `spiralSample`, `helixSample`, `ellipseSample` (accuracy vs analytical, tolerance 1e-6).
  - `offsetPolyline` (convex + concave).
- **Integration tests** (`__tests__/drawing/stair-tool.test.tsx`): simulate click + dynamic input ŌåÆ asserts scene + command history.
- **Visual regression** (ADR-343): snapshot per ogni kind in stato default.
- **Property-based tests** (fast-check): `2R + G` rule, walkline length consistency, geometry self-intersection check.

---

## 9. Q&A ŌĆö Round 1 (Q1-Q16) risolti, Round 2 (Q17-Q34) in corso

### 9.1 Round 1 ŌĆö risolti 2026-05-16

| # | Tema | Decisione |
|---|---|---|
| Q1 | Unit├Ā di misura | **Entrambe switchabili**. Default `cm`, canonico interno mm. Formatter/parser SSoT. |
| Q2 | Modalit├Ā disegno | **Ibrida**. Ribbon contextual panel sticky + 2-click placement con preview live. |
| Q3 | Tipologie prioritarie | **TUTTE 10** (completeness over MVP). |
| Q4 | Code profile | Tutti disponibili, default `NOK`. Override per-stair + per-progetto. |
| Q5 | Validator behavior | **Ibrido**. Hard errors bloccano, code violations warn non-bloccanti. |
| Q6 | Walkline visibility | Industry-aligned: ORATA during draw/edit, NASCOSTA dopo. Toggle on-demand. |
| Q7 | Arrow label | i18n locale-driven (`╬æ╬Ø╬® 16 ╬▓╬▒╬Ė╬╝╬»╬┤╬ĄŽé` / `UP 16 risers`). |
| Q8 | Editing post-creazione | **Entrambi**: contextual ribbon tab + floating Advanced Properties panel. |
| Q9 | Curve input | **Entrambe modalit├Ā** (inner+width OR inner+outer), 3 campi sincronizzati. |
| Q10 | Winder methods | **Tutti 4** (equal-going, kite, balanced, pie). |
| Q11 | Firestore | **Nuova collection `floorplan_stairs`** (industry-aligned IfcStair). |
| Q12 | "Triangolare" | **3 interpretazioni coperte**: `winder.method=kite` + `triangular-fan` + `triangular-outline`. |
| Q13 | Sketch mode | **MVP (Phase 4)**. Completeness over MVP. |
| Q14 | NOK subtype default | Toggle ╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒/╬┤╬ĄŽģŽä╬ĄŽü╬ĄŽŹ╬┐ŽģŽā╬▒ in panel, default `╬║ŽŹŽü╬╣╬▒`. |
| Q15 | Ribbon variants timing | **Tutte 10 live dal merge** (no comingSoon). |
| Q16 | ADR number | **358** confermato. |

### 9.2 Round 2 ŌĆö Q17-Q34 (in attesa di risposta Giorgio, 2026-05-16)

| # | Tema | Stato | Decisione |
|---|------|-------|-----------|
| Q17 | Multi-storey: `totalRise` auto da altezza piano (`multiStoryConfig`) o sempre raw input? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Entrambi (╬│)**. Default raw `totalRise` manuale. Se utente collega `multiStoryConfig.topLevel` a un level del project ŌåÆ `totalRise` diventa COMPUTED da `storyHeight ├Ś storyCount`, raw input disabilitato. Cambio level height ŌåÆ tutte le stair collegate ricalcolano automaticamente. |
| Q18 | `structureType`: tutti 8 tipi (monolithic/stringer/cantilever/spine/suspended/glass/grating) Phase 1, o solo monolithic + others Phase 9? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Tutti 8 (╬▒)**. Full enterprise / completeness over MVP. Phase 1 implementa render 2D per tutti i `structureType`. Stringer-* render con polyline bold. Cantilever/suspended/glass-tread/steel-grating in 2D = sola variazione di stroke style + symbol; 3D-completo Phase 9. |
| Q19 | Materials/finishes: solo per-stair default, o anche per-tread override (ArchiCAD pattern)? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Default per-stair + per-tread override (╬▓)**. Full ArchiCAD enterprise. `params.materials.{tread,riser,stringer,landing}` = default per-stair. `params.perTreadOverrides[treadIndex].material` = override singolo. Edit mode: select stair ŌåÆ enter Tread Edit Mode ŌåÆ click singolo tread ŌåÆ property panel mostra override material/nosing/customProfile. Senza override ŌåÆ eredita default. |
| Q20 | `riserType` (open/closed): param indipendente, o derivato da `structureType`? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Smart default + override (╬│)**. Industry convergence (ArchiCAD/Revit/AutoCAD Arch/Vectorworks): `riserType` ├© param indipendente ma con default auto-suggerito da `structureType`. Default mapping: monolithic/stringer-*ŌåÆ`closed`; cantilever/suspended/glass-tread/steel-gratingŌåÆ`open`. User pu├▓ override liberamente (es. monolithic + open per LED understep). |
| Q21 | `cutPlaneHeight`: default fisso 1200mm, o configurabile per-progetto (project setting)? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Project default + per-stair override (╬┤)**. Project setting `dxf:project.cutPlaneHeight` (default 1200mm). `StairParams.cutPlaneHeight?` opzionale = se assente eredita project; se presente override per-stair. UI: contextual ribbon panel mostra "Inherit from project (1200mm)" toggle. |
| Q22 | Edit grips: tutti 5 tipi (basePoint/direction/width/length/split) Phase 5, o solo basePoint+direction Phase 5 e altri Phase 9? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Tutti 5 grips Phase 5 (╬│)**. Industry convergence (Revit/ArchiCAD/BricsCAD) + completeness over MVP. `splitGrip` attivo solo per kind Ōłł {l-shape, u-shape, gamma}. Implementazione riusa overlay grip system di line tool ADR-357. Snap+ortho+polar attivi durante drag. |
| Q23 | Mirror semantica: `mirrorStairParams` inverte automaticamente `turnDirection`/`turnSequence`, o user toggle manuale? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Auto-flip (╬│ŌåÆ╬▒)**. `mirrorStairParams(params, axis)` inverte automaticamente `turnDirection` (cwŌåöccw, leftŌåöright) e `turnSequence[]` array. Evita Revit bug noto (perdita parametricit├Ā post-mirror). Zero azione utente. Stesso comportamento per `rotateStairParams` quando angolo=180┬░. |
| Q24 | Auto landing depth: default `'auto'` (= width) o numero fisso (es. 1200mm)? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Default `'auto'` = width (╬│ŌåÆ╬▒)**. Industry-aligned (Revit/ArchiCAD/Vectorworks). NOK-compliant by construction (NOK: landing Ōēź width). Override manuale possibile; se `landingDepth < width` validator emette warning non-bloccante "╬Ā╬╗╬▒ŽäŽŹŽā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ < ŽĆ╬╗╬¼Žä╬┐ŽģŽé Žā╬║╬¼╬╗╬▒Žé ŌĆö ╬Ø╬¤╬Ü violation" + badge rosso. Min suggerita nel UI = `width` quando `codeProfile='nok'`. |
| Q25 | Code profiles aggiuntivi: tutti 9 (NOK/IBC/Eurocode/NBC/NFPA/AS1657/DIN/ADA/none) immediatamente, o solo NOK+IBC+Eurocode (round 1) + altri Phase 6.5+? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **NOK+IBC+Eurocode+ADA Phase 6 (╬│)**. ADA ├© critico per export USA (mercato con accessibility legalmente vincolante). NBC/NFPA/AS1657/DIN restano placeholder type-only (Phase 9 o on-demand). `gate-stair-checker.ts` Phase 6 implementa 4 validators: NOK, IBC, Eurocode, ADA. ADA validator copre: variation step Ōēż4.8mm, handrail height 864-965mm, topExtension Ōēź305mm, bottomExtension = 1 tread, contrast strip presence. |
| Q26 | ADA handrail extensions (top 305mm, bottom one-tread): render Phase 1, o solo validator Phase 6.5? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **All Phase 6 coherent ship (╬│ŌåÆ╬▓)**. Render extensions + validator + auto-default `topExtension=305mm`/`bottomExtension='one-tread'` quando `codeProfile='ada'` insieme. Type fields esistenti gi├Ā in Phase 1, ma UI exposure + render solo da Phase 6. ADA ├© un pacchetto completo, non frammentato. |
| Q27 | Egress `occupancyLoad`: opzionale per-stair, o ereditato da setting per-progetto? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Project default + per-stair override (╬│)**. Stesso pattern di Q21. Project setting `dxf:project.occupancyLoad` (default `null`=disabilitato). `StairParams.occupancyLoad?` opzionale: se assente eredita project; se presente override per-stair. UI: contextual ribbon mostra "Inherit from project (N persons)" toggle. Validator emette warning se `width < occupancyLoad ├Ś 7.62`. |
| Q28 | Tread numbering default: `display='all'` visibile in plan, `'nth'` ogni N, o `'none'`? Restart per flight default ON? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **`display='all'` + restart OFF (╬│)**. Industry convergence (Revit/ArchiCAD/AutoCAD Arch/Vectorworks): default tutti i tread numerati, numerazione continua 1ŌåÆN attraverso landing (no restart per flight). QTO-friendly (total count visibile). User override per-stair: `'nth'` (con `nthStep` param, default 5) o `'none'`. Restart per flight = opzionale toggle nel property panel (default OFF, industry standard construction drawings). |
| Q29 | Headroom check: real-time durante draw (debounced), o solo post-creation batch? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Hybrid (╬│)**. Real-time cheap check (debounced 300ms): 2D overlap test con entities su layer `*ceiling*` / `*slab*` ŌåÆ flash warning giallo "╬ł╬╗╬Ą╬│╬Š╬Ą headroom" senza raycast. Post-creation full batch validator: `verticalDistance < minHeadroom(codeProfile)` ŌåÆ red badge nel property panel. Phase 9 (3D): full raycast real-time. Industry-aligned (Revit real-time / ArchiCAD post / Vectorworks hybrid) + performance-friendly per 2D plan view. |
| Q30 | Schedule/QTO export formats: CSV+Excel+PDF tutti Phase 8.5, o solo CSV Phase 8.5 + Excel/PDF Phase 9? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Tutti 3 formats Phase 8.5 (╬▓)**. Completeness over MVP + industry convergence (Revit/ArchiCAD/AutoCAD Arch tutti esportano CSV+Excel+PDF Day 1). Stack: `exceljs` (MIT) per .xlsx, `pdfmake` (MIT) per PDF tabular, native JS per CSV. Unico `generateScheduleData()` factory + 3 small writers. License check Ō£ģ (entrambe MIT). |
| Q31 | Hotkey `'st'`: OK o preferisci altra lettera? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **`'st'` confermato (╬▒)**. Mnemonic da **st**air + industry convergence (AutoCAD `STAIR/ST`, ArchiCAD `'st'`, Bricsys BIM `STAIR/ST` ŌĆö 3/4 major vendors). Zero conflict con 11 existing hotkeys Nestor DXF tool. Riserva `'se'`/`'sm'` per future stair-edit/stair-mirror tools. |
| Q32 | Library presets scope: tutti 3 (user/company/project) Phase 7.5, o solo company Phase 7.5? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Tutti 3 scopes Phase 7.5 (╬▓)**. Completeness over MVP + industry convergence (Revit Types/Families, ArchiCAD Favorites 3-level, Vectorworks Resource Manager ŌĆö 3/3 vendors). Schema: unica collection `stair_presets` con `scope: 'user'|'company'|'project'` + `ownerId` + `companyId` + `projectId?`. Firestore rules: 3 read + 3 write rules basate su tenant isolation ADR-294/ADR-356. UI: 3 grouped sections in dropdown. Cost Day-1 vs retrofit = 3x risparmio. |
| Q33 | Anti-clash con muri/colonne: confermare out-of-scope Phase 1-8 (industry standard)? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Out-of-scope confermato Phase 1-8 (╬▒)**. Industry convergence 5/6 vendor (Revit/ArchiCAD/AutoCAD Arch/Vectorworks/BricsCAD): wall/column clash = 3D-only feature (Navisworks/Clash Detective). Motivi: (1) perf real-time intersection in draw loop, (2) semantic ambiguity 2D senza level metadata = false positives, (3) headroom check Q29 gi├Ā copre vertical clash. Visual-only in Phase 1-8 (user vede e giudica). Phase 9+ riusa raycast 3D pipeline per anti-clash completo. Gi├Ā documentato ┬¦3.9. |
| Q34 | Custom step profile (`nosingSide`): solo `'front'` Phase 1, o anche `'front-and-sides'`? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-16 | **Entrambi `'front'` + `'front-and-sides'` Phase 1 (╬▓)**. Coerenza con Q18 (╬▓): tutti 8 `structureType` Phase 1 includono cantilever/glass-tread/steel-grating che richiedono `'front-and-sides'` per render corretto. Smart default per `structureType`: monolithic/stringer-* ŌåÆ `'front'`; cantilever/glass-tread/steel-grating ŌåÆ `'front-and-sides'`. Per-stair override + per-tread override (Q19). Industry alignment con enterprise tier (ArchiCAD/AutoCAD Arch/Allplan 3/6). Completeness over MVP. |
| Q35 | Strict mode quando `linkedToFloor`: derived stepCount + hard error overflow/underflow + length grip clamp, oppure soft warning + free edit (Phase 9 baseline)? | Ō£ģ resolved 2026-05-17 | **Strict mode (╬│ŌåÆ╬▓)**. Industry convergence 5/5 (Revit "Desired Riser Height" + ArchiCAD Story Sensitive + AutoCAD Architecture `bindToLevels` + Vectorworks story snap + BricsCAD BIMSTAIR). Quando `linkedToFloor === true`: `stepCount = round(storyHeight ├Ś storyCount / rise)` (derived), `totalRise = storyHeight ├Ś storyCount` (locked). User edit su `rise` ŌåÆ stepCount auto. User edit su `stepCount` ŌåÆ rise auto-derived (inverse). Length grip clamp a `tread ├Ś (maxStepCount ŌłÆ 1)` + magnet snap a maxRun nel 10% finale. Overflow/underflow emettono `hardError.totalRiseOverFloor` / `hardError.totalRiseUnderFloor` (red), routed via `hardErrors` field a `StairWarningsSection`. Free mode (`linkedToFloor !== true`) resta come Phase 7a (warning soft + edit libero). Helper SSoT `systems/stairs/stair-floor-link.ts` (`reconcileLinkedStair` pure + idempotent). Implementato Phase 9B-2. |

| 2026-07-10 | **┬¦Phase 8 ŌĆö hover halo ╬▒╬║╬┐╬╗╬┐Žģ╬Ė╬Ą╬» Žä╬┐ ╬Ā╬Ī╬æ╬ō╬£╬æ╬ż╬Ö╬Ü╬¤ ╬▒ŽĆ╬┐ŽäŽŹŽĆŽē╬╝╬▒ (Giorgio: ┬½╬ō Žā╬║╬¼╬╗╬▒ ŌåÆ ╬ō ŽĆ╬ĄŽü╬»╬│Žü╬▒╬╝╬╝╬▒, ŽīŽć╬╣ Žä╬ĄŽäŽü╬¼╬│Žē╬Į╬┐┬╗).** Bug: Žä╬┐ hover/highlight glow ╬╝╬╣╬▒Žé L/U/╬ō Žā╬║╬¼╬╗╬▒Žé ╬«Žä╬▒╬Į **╬┐Žü╬Ė╬┐╬│ŽÄ╬Į╬╣╬┐ OBB** (`drawPerimeterOutline` ŌåÆ oriented bounding box) ŽĆ╬┐Žģ ŽĆ╬ĄŽü╬╣╬Ł╬║╬╗╬Ą╬╣╬Ą Žä╬Ę╬Į **╬║╬Ą╬Į╬« ╬ĄŽāŽēŽä╬ĄŽü╬╣╬║╬« ╬│Žē╬Į╬»╬▒** Žä╬┐Žģ ╬ō. SSoT scoperta critica: `StairNokSubType` esisteva gi├Ā con 2 valori `'main' \| 'secondary'` e `gateStairChecker.checkNOK` gi├Ā branchava `widthMin = isMain ? 1200 : 900` ŌĆö quindi **estendere il sistema esistente invece di duplicare** (N.0/N.12). Type extension (`types/stair.ts`): `StairNokSubType` passa a `'main' \| 'low-rise' \| 'internal' \| 'auxiliary' \| 'secondary'` (legacy `'secondary'` mantenuto come alias deprecato per back-compat); `StairValidationState.comfortViolations?: readonly string[]` aggiunto per yellow band soft warnings. Engine (`gate-stair-checker.ts`): 2 nuove SSoT tables `NOK_WIDTH_LEGAL_MIN_MM` (1200/900/600/600) + `NOK_WIDTH_COMFORT_MIN_MM` (1200/1000/800/600) ŌĆö sotto legal = red `nok.widthMin`, tra legal e comfort = yellow `nok.widthBelowComfort` (dual-tier choice ╬Æ decisa da Giorgio 2026-05-17 Q&A in greco). Rise/tread/2R+G envelope continuano a usare lo split strict main vs relaxed others (╬Ø╬¤╬Ü non subdivide rise/tread per scope, solo width). `GateStairCheckerResult.comfortViolations` nuovo campo + `dispatchProfile` ritorna 3-tuple. Validator wrapper (`stair-validator.ts`): propaga `comfortViolations` come optional spread nel `StairValidationState` (disjoint da `violationKeys` ŌĆö il count `hasCodeViolations` NON include comfort). Persistence (`useStairPersistence.hydrateLegacyParams`): hydration step extends Phase 3f shim ŌĆö legacy `nokSubType: 'secondary'` viene riscritto a `'low-rise'` (stessa min legale 0.90 m, semantica pi├╣ chiara). UI ribbon (Q3 user choice ╬Æ: dentro panel "╬ö╬┐╬╝╬« / ╬ŻŽć╬«╬╝╬▒" esistente, non panel separato): nuovo command key `STAIR_RIBBON_KEYS.stringParams.nokSubType` + read helper (defaults legacy `'secondary'` a `'low-rise'`, `null`-safe per non-NOK profiles via fallback `'main'`) + patch helper `patchNokSubType` (normalizza `'secondary'` ŌåÆ `'low-rise'` on write, valida via `VALID_NOK_SUB_TYPES` set, no-op quando uguale). `contextual-stair-tab.ts`: nuovo `NOK_SUB_TYPE_OPTIONS` (4 opzioni i18n routed) + 4┬░ combobox nel panel `stair-structure` (180px, dopo riserType). i18n el+en `dxf-viewer-shell.json`: nuova sezione `ribbon.commands.stairEditor.nokSubType.{section.title, main, lowRise, internal, auxiliary}` ŌĆö greco puro ("╬Ü╬Ą╬ĮŽäŽü╬╣╬║Žī ╬Ü╬╗╬╣╬╝╬▒╬║╬┐ŽāŽä╬¼Žā╬╣╬┐" / "╬ÜŽä╬»Žü╬╣╬┐ ╬ŁŽēŽé 3 ╬┐ŽüŽīŽå╬┐ŽģŽé" / "╬ĢŽāŽēŽä╬ĄŽü╬╣╬║╬« ╬Ż╬║╬¼╬╗╬▒ ╬Ü╬▒Žä╬┐╬╣╬║╬»╬▒Žé" / "╬Æ╬┐╬Ę╬Ė╬ĘŽä╬╣╬║╬« ╬Ż╬║╬¼╬╗╬▒"); `tool-hints.json` el+en: nuova chiave `tools.stair.validator.nok.widthBelowComfort` ("╬ż╬┐ ŽĆ╬╗╬¼Žä╬┐Žé ╬Ą╬»╬Į╬▒╬╣ ╬ĮŽī╬╝╬╣╬╝╬┐ ╬▒╬╗╬╗╬¼ ŽāŽä╬Ą╬ĮŽī ╬│╬╣╬▒ ╬¼╬Į╬ĄŽä╬Ę ŽćŽü╬«Žā╬Ę." / "Width is legal but tight for comfortable use."). | 2026-05-17 | **Phase 3f IMPLEMENTED ŌĆö L-shape with NOK-compliant winders (cornerStyle discriminator + Phase 3e split-grip regression fix)**. Giorgio request: ribbon kind switch to "╬ŻŽć╬«╬╝╬▒Žä╬┐Žé ╬ō" produced only the ŽĆ╬╗╬▒ŽäŽŹŽā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ variant; user needed the alternative NOK-standard option with **Žā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ŽĆ╬¼Žä╬╣╬▒ ╬║╬┐ŽģŽü╬╝ŽĆ╬▒Žü╬╣ŽāŽä╬¼** (winder treads) at the corner that preserve walkline going (arc-length / winderCount = standard going). Industry research 5/5 (Revit "Run Type" sub-selector / ArchiCAD "Winder Method" / AutoCAD Architecture "Winders" toggle / Vectorworks "Corner Type" / BricsCAD BIMSTAIR corner option): all 5 vendors surface the choice as a **sub-option** within the L-shape kind, because the footprint is still a quarter-turn L ŌĆö only the corner detail differs. Design: `StairVariantLShape` becomes a TypeScript discriminated union on `cornerStyle: 'landing' \| 'winders'` (`StairVariantLShapeLanding` / `StairVariantLShapeWinders`) with two type-guard helpers exported. Count conservation invariants: landing variant `n1 + 1(landing) + n2 = stepCount`; winders variant `n1 + winderCount + n2 = stepCount` ŌĆö both preserve `totalRise = stepCount ┬Ę rise`, so the kind switch and the sub-style toggle leave the user's total numbered surfaces unchanged. Defaults (NOK quarter-turn standard): `winderCount: 3`, `winderMethod: 'equal-going'` (walkline-preserving; `'pie'` available as alternative, `'kite'`/`'balanced'` still throw Phase 4c sentinel). SSoT reuse ŌĆö zero geometry duplication: the new `computeLShapeWithWinders` calls directly into `stair-geometry-winder.ts` helpers (`buildWinderLayout`, `buildWinderFlight1`, `buildWinderTreads`, `buildWinderFlight2`, `buildWinderWalkline`, `winderTangentAt`, `rotateVec` ŌĆö all promoted from `function` to `export function`); `buildWinderLayout` refactored to accept caller-supplied `n1`/`n2` (l-shape passes user-controlled `flightSplit`, winder kind keeps its symmetric auto-split via `Math.floor((stepCount ŌłÆ winderCount)/2)` at the caller site). Winders are emitted into `geometry.treads` as `'tread'`-kind labels (NOT landings ŌĆö they are walkable steps) so `buildTreadLabels` (no-landings variant) is the correct labeler; `geometry.landings: []` for winders variant. Ribbon: new contextual panel `stair-corner` (visibilityKey `lShapeCorner` ŌĆö visible iff `variant.kind === 'l-shape'`) with the `cornerStyle` combobox; sibling panel `stair-corner-winders` (visibilityKey `lShapeWindersParams` ŌĆö gated by both `kind === 'l-shape'` AND `cornerStyle === 'winders'`) hosts `winderCount` (1-5 combobox) + `winderMethod` (equal-going / pie). Split into 2 panels because `RibbonPanelDef.visibilityKey` is panel-scoped, not button-scoped. Bridge: 3 new command keys (`cornerStyle`, `winderMethod`, `winderCount`) + 2 visibility keys added to `STAIR_RIBBON_KEYS` / `STAIR_RIBBON_VISIBILITY_KEYS`; `readStairStringField`/`readStairNumericField` narrow `variant.kind === 'l-shape'` (+ optional `cornerStyle === 'winders'` for winder fields); 3 new patch helpers (`patchLShapeCornerStyle`, `patchLShapeWinderMethod`, `patchLShapeWinderCount`) ŌĆö corner-style toggle rebuilds the variant via factory (`buildLShapeWindersVariant` or `buildDefaultVariantFor('l-shape', ...)` landing default, both preserving `turnDirection`); winderCount edit clamps `[1, min(5, stepCount ŌłÆ 2)]` and recomputes `flightSplit` via `splitTwoFlightsForWinders(stepCount, winderCount)`. Persistence: `useStairPersistence.docToEntity` runs new `hydrateLegacyParams` shim that maps legacy l-shape docs without `cornerStyle` ŌåÆ `cornerStyle: 'landing'` (zero migration cost). **Phase 3e split-grip regression caught + fixed**: `stair-grips.withFlightSplitStepCounts` was still asserting `n1 + n2 === stepCount` for l-shape/u-shape/gamma even after Phase 3e introduced the ╬│ landing convention (`n1 + n2 = stepCount ŌłÆ 1` / `stepCount ŌłÆ 2`); split-grip drags therefore silently broke count conservation. The function now branches on `cornerStyle` for l-shape (`stepCount ŌłÆ 1` for landing, `stepCount ŌłÆ winderCount` for winders), `stepCount ŌłÆ 1` for u-shape, `stepCount ŌłÆ 2` for gamma. Test 9 in `stair-grips.test.ts` updated to assert the correct expected total per variant. i18n el+en: `ribbon.panels.stairCorner` ("╬ōŽē╬Į╬»╬▒" / "Corner") + `stairCornerWinders` ("╬Ż╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ŽĆ╬¼Žä╬╣╬▒ ╬ōŽē╬Į╬»╬▒Žé" / "Corner Winders") + `ribbon.commands.stairEditor.cornerStyle.{section.title, landing, winders}` ("╬żŽŹŽĆ╬┐Žé ╬ōŽē╬Į╬»╬▒Žé / ╬Ā╬╗╬▒ŽäŽŹŽā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ / ╬Ż╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ŽĆ╬¼Žä╬╣╬▒") + `winderCount.section.title` ("╬æŽü╬╣╬Ė╬╝ŽīŽé ╬Ż╬║╬▒╬╗╬╣ŽÄ╬Į ╬ōŽē╬Į╬»╬▒Žé") + `winderMethod.{section.title, equalGoing, pie}` ("╬£╬Ł╬Ė╬┐╬┤╬┐Žé ╬ōŽē╬Į╬»╬▒Žé / ╬ÖŽāŽīŽĆ╬╗╬▒Žä╬┐ ╬Ā╬¼Žä╬Ę╬╝╬▒ / ╬żŽü╬»╬│Žē╬Į╬▒") ŌĆö zero `defaultValue` literals (SOS N.11), pure Greek shape descriptors. Tests: NEW `__tests__/StairGeometryService-lshape-winders.test.ts` (15 tests): tread count + landings:[] invariant, contiguous z-progression (no extra rise), flight1/winders/flight2 vertex projections per turn direction, walkline 6-vertex shape (base + winderCount+1 arc samples + flight2 end), stringer presence, cutLine emission, treadLabels all `kind === 'tread'`, left/right turn mirroring, winderCount=2 minimum, `'pie'` method 3-vertex polygons, bbox spans both legs, total rise = `stepCount ┬Ę rise`. `stair-variant-defaults.test.ts` +6 tests (default cornerStyle, `buildLShapeWindersVariant` NOK seeds, turnDirection preservation, `splitTwoFlightsForWinders` edge cases). All 4 legacy l-shape test setups updated with `cornerStyle: 'landing'` (mandatory in discriminated union). **313/313 stair suite PASS** (292 Phase 3e baseline + 6 variant-defaults + 15 lshape-winders = +21). Out of scope: u-shape and gamma with winders (future Phase 3g/3h, same SSoT extension pattern); `'kite'` / `'balanced'` winder methods; drawing landings as filled polygons (renderer unchanged ŌĆö winders are in `geometry.treads` so they paint as fills automatically). User can now toggle ŽĆ╬╗╬▒ŽäŽŹŽā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ Ōåö Žā╬║╬▒╬╗╬┐ŽĆ╬¼Žä╬╣╬▒ from the ribbon without losing turnDirection, stepCount, or any geometry parameters. |
| 2026-05-17 | **Phase 3e IMPLEMENTED ŌĆö Numbering Convention ╬│ + Cut-Plane Filter (renderer SSoT fix)**. Bug surfaced after Phase 3d Kind Selector reached the ribbon: a straight stair drawn at rise=100/stepCount=17 displayed 17 tread numbers; switching kind to "╬ŻŽć╬«╬╝╬▒Žä╬┐Žé ╬ō" (l-shape) silently dropped to 11 numbers (loss of 6) and the landing carried no label. Three intertwined defects identified: (a) `StairRenderer.drawTreadLabels` iterated `treadsBelowCut` with `start + i` ignoring the SSoT `geometry.treadLabels` populated by the factory ŌĆö so `treadLabelRestartPerFlight` was honored at compute-time but obliterated at render-time, and `cutPlaneHeight` filtering was an accidental side effect of `treadsBelowCut.length` rather than an explicit pass; (b) `computeLShape`/`computeUShape`/`computeGamma` emitted landings into `geometry.landings` but never produced a label for them, leaving plan-view landings unnumbered against AutoCAD/Revit convention ╬│; (c) `buildDefaultVariantFor('l-shape'/'u-shape')` factory used `splitTwoFlights(stepCount)` summing to `stepCount` (e.g. 17 ŌåÆ [8,9]) ŌĆö so the l-shape geometry produced 17 treads + 1 landing = 18 numberable surfaces, breaking count-conservation across kind switches even though the underlying z-model already consumes 1 rise per landing (`(n1+n2+1)┬Ęrise`). Decisions confirmed with Giorgio (Greek Q&A, 2026-05-17): convention **(╬│)** ŌĆö landing carries its own number, conserving total numbered surfaces = `stepCount`; cut-plane filter **(╬▒)** ŌĆö AutoCAD/Revit/ArchiCAD standard hides labels above the cut plane (labels-above-cut culled at render time). Two new factory helpers added: `splitTwoFlightsWithLanding(stepCount)` splits `(stepCount - 1)` so `n1 + landing(1) + n2 = stepCount`, and `splitThreeFlightsWithLandings(stepCount)` splits `(stepCount - 2)` for gamma's 2 landings ŌĆö both clamp Ōēź1 per flight. `StairTreadLabel` gained an optional `kind?: 'tread' \| 'landing'` discriminator (back-compat ŌĆö omitted means 'tread'). New SSoT helper `buildTreadLabelsWithLandings(treads, landings, flightSplit, ...)` in `stair-geometry-labels.ts` interleaves a landing label between each pair of flights (`treadIndex = treadCursor`, `position = centroid3D(landing)`, `kind: 'landing'`); the existing `buildTreadLabels` stays in place for kinds without landings (straight, v-shape, winder, spiral, helical, elliptical, sketch, triangular-*). Renderer rewrite (`StairRenderer.drawTreadLabels`, ~30 LOC ŌåÆ fits Google SRP): reads `geometry.treadLabels` directly, skips any label with `position.z >= (params.cutPlaneHeight ?? DEFAULT_CUT_PLANE_HEIGHT)`, renders text at the label's stored centroid ŌĆö `'nth'` filtering already applied factory-side so the render pass no longer duplicates that logic. Files: `stair-variant-defaults.ts` (+2 helpers exported, 3 factory branches re-pointed), `types/stair.ts` (+1 optional field), `stair-geometry-labels.ts` (+1 new fn ~50 LOC), `stair-geometry-lshape.ts` / `stair-geometry-ushape.ts` / `stair-geometry-gamma.ts` (call site swapped ŌĆö 1 line each), `rendering/entities/StairRenderer.ts` (drawTreadLabels rewrite + `DEFAULT_CUT_PLANE_HEIGHT` import). Tests: +6 in `stair-variant-defaults.test.ts` (helpers: `splitTwoFlightsWithLanding(17)===[8,8]`, `splitThreeFlightsWithLandings(17)` sum=15, edge clamps, count-conservation invariant), Test 2/3 updated for the new sum semantic; lshape continuous + restart-per-flight label tests in `tread-labels.test.ts` updated to assert the landing label at index 5 with `kind === 'landing'` and continuous numbering (`['1'..'11']` instead of `['1'..'10']`); `StairGeometryService-ushape.test.ts` Test 10/11 + `StairGeometryService-gamma.test.ts` Test 10/11 updated for ╬│ counts (11 labels for u-shape stepCount=10 split [5,5], 12 for gamma split [3,4,3]). All 292/292 stair suite PASS. Outcome on the reported regression (mm scene, rise=100, stepCount=17): factory now produces `[8,8]` so flight1(8) + landing(1) + flight2(z=900,1000,1100 ŌåÆ 3 below 1200mm cut) = **12 visible numbers** (1-12), 13-17 hidden above cut (╬▒), total numberable surfaces = 17 (╬│ count conservation across kind switch). V-shape unaffected (no landing ŌĆö keeps `splitTwoFlights`). Out of scope: drawing the landing polygon as a filled shape (renderer still doesn't paint `geometry.landings` ŌĆö only the label centroid is now placed on it); risers numbering; user-facing cut-plane filter toggle. |

| 2026-05-17 | **Phase 3d HOTFIX-1 ŌĆö flightSplit ratioŌåÆstepcount + L/U/╬ō arrow on flight 1**. Two latent bugs surfaced the moment Phase 3d Kind Selector made L-shape/U-shape/Gamma reachable from the ribbon. (a) `stair-grips.withFlightSplitRatio` wrote `flightSplit: [r, 1-r]` as a 0-1 ratio, but every geometry builder (`buildLShapeFlight1` et al.) reads `flightSplit[i]` as integer step count and calls `new Array(n_i)` ŌĆö float input throws `RangeError: invalid array length` as soon as the user touches the split grip. Renamed helper ŌåÆ `withFlightSplitStepCounts(variant, r, stepCount)`: rounds `r┬ĘstepCount` to an integer in `[1, stepCount-1]` and derives the second flight as `stepCount - n1`, guaranteeing `n1 + n2 === stepCount` and `n_i Ōēź 1`. Gamma extends to 3-flight with `[n1, floor(rem/2), rem - floor(rem/2)]`. (b) Arrow symbol on L/U/╬ō stairs drew a straight diagonal from `basePoint` to `walkline[last]` ŌĆö for multi-flight stairs this cut visually across the L/U/╬ō corner. Now `arrow = arrowSymbol(walkline[0], walkline[1], upDirection)` so the UP indicator sits on flight 1, matching AutoCAD/Revit/ArchiCAD plan-view convention (UP arrow on flight 1, multi-flight ascent implied by tread numbering past the landing). 3 builder files patched (`stair-geometry-lshape.ts`, `stair-geometry-ushape.ts`, `stair-geometry-gamma.ts`); V-shape arrow already correct (apex ŌåÆ arm 1 tip). Tests updated: `StairGeometryService-lshape.test.ts:Test 10` now asserts `arrow.start = walkline[0]` + `arrow.end = walkline[1]`; `stair-grips.test.ts:Test 9` asserts integer step counts summing to `stepCount` (was: float in `[0.1, 0.9]` summing to 1). 286/286 stair suite PASS after the fix. |

| 2026-05-17 | **Phase Q17 9B-6 HOTFIX ŌĆö freshly drawn stair flickered in then disappeared**. Two-part fix: (a) `useStairPersistence` diff-merge now preserves local stairs that have never been persisted (`!lastSavedParamsRef.current.has(id)`) in addition to in-flight dirty stairs. Without this guard, a stair placed via the tool was added to the local scene, then the next Firestore snapshot fired before `floorplan_stairs/{id}` round-tripped ŌĆö the diff-merge saw "in scene but not in docs" and dropped it (mutated=true ŌåÆ scene rewritten without the stair). Pairs with the diff-merge preserve so the optimistic local entity survives until the save completes, then the snapshot picks up the persisted doc cleanly. Industry pattern 5/5 (Revit transaction commit + Firestore optimistic UI + Google Docs immediate-save). Zero new state, two-file fix (~16 LOC). |

| 2026-05-17 | **Phase 9B-2 IMPLEMENTED ŌĆö strict floor-bound stair mode (Q35)**. NEW SSoT module `systems/stairs/stair-floor-link.ts` (`reconcileLinkedStair` pure + idempotent, `maxStepCountFor` / `minStepCountFor` code-aware bounds, `deriveRiseFromStepCount` inverse, exported `mmFactorFromWidth` heuristic) ŌĆö Tier-3 candidate; existing `mmFactorFromWidth` copies in `stair-validator` / `stair-auto-fix` / `stair-grips` remain for now (TODO follow-up to consolidate via `resolveSceneUnits` SSoT, ADR-358 Phase 8). `useRibbonStairBridge` patch helpers wire reconcile: `patchRise` calls `reconcileLinkedStair(withRecomputedTotals(...))` so rise is the primary lever; `patchStepCount` inverts when linked (`deriveRiseFromStepCount` ŌåÆ rewrite rise ŌåÆ reconcile) so stepCount lands exactly on the envelope (Revit "Desired Riser Height" pattern). `stair-grips.resizeLength` clamps the length grip to `tread ├Ś (maxStepCount ŌłÆ 1)` (scene units) and magnet-snaps at the last 10% of `maxRun` (Revit / ArchiCAD "magnet to top level"); `totalRise` is locked to `storyHeight ├Ś storyCount`. `stair-completion.buildDefaultStairParams` reconciles post-build so a stair placed on a 3000mm floor with default 175mm rise lands on `stepCount = 17` out of the box (instead of seeded 12). `stair-validator.checkStoryHeightOverflow` + `checkStoryHeightUnderflow` emit `hardError.totalRiseOverFloor` / `hardError.totalRiseUnderFloor` when linked (red box) instead of the soft `totalRiseOver/BelowStoryHeight` (orange); both are appended to the `hardErrors` field so `StairWarningsSection.partitionViolations` routes them correctly. `stair-auto-fix.autoFixStairParams` reconciles BEFORE the code-range fixes so "Auto-fix" on a linked stair never reintroduces overflow. NEW unit suite `__tests__/stair-floor-link.test.ts` (26/26 PASS): mmFactor heuristic, code-aware step bounds, inverse helpers, no-op cases, mm/cm/m scene-unit conversions, idempotency (apply-twice = same ref). i18n hard-error keys `tools.stair.validator.hardError.totalRiseOverFloor` + `tools.stair.validator.hardError.totalRiseUnderFloor` added el+en (no `defaultValue` literals per SOS N.11). risers between consecutive treads as `Segment3D` vertical edge (stepCount-1); walkline = 2-vertex polyline (basePoint ŌåÆ +u┬Ętread┬Ę(stepCount-1), z linear 0..(stepCount-1)┬Ęrise); stringers = `offsetPolyline(walkline, ┬▒width/2)`;
